# Scan Report: London

- Issue: https://github.com/mgifford/open-scans/issues/68
- Submitted by: mgifford
- Scanned at: 2026-03-14T01:07:01.094Z
- Engines used: AXE, ALFA
- Scan duration: 17.4 minutes
- Total URLs submitted: 100
- Accepted public URLs: 100
- Rejected URLs: 0
- 🌙 **Dark mode tested: 26 of 100 URLs (26%) support `prefers-color-scheme: dark`**
- ALFA outcomes: 126853 passed, 2326 failed, 14277 cantTell, 5158 inapplicable
- axe outcomes: 78843 passed, 174 failed, 217 cantTell, 6233 inapplicable
- Equal Access outcomes: 0 passed, 0 failed (0 unique, 0 duplicate), 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- AccessLint outcomes: 0 passed, 0 failed (0 unique, 0 duplicate), 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- QualWeb outcomes: 0 passed, 0 failed, 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- Duplicate findings caught by later scanners: 1391

## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 68 page(s) - 68 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<button class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link">...</button>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://london.gov.uk/
- https://london.gov.uk/warmer-homes-faqs/i-received-support-under-first-phase-warmer-homes-can-i-re-apply-phase-warmer-homes
- https://london.gov.uk/find-affordable-home
- https://london.gov.uk/find-your-london-festival
- https://london.gov.uk/what-affordable-home-and-how-can-i-find-one
- *...and 63 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 2: Affects 68 page(s) - 68 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**Issue**: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<p>© Copyright Greater London Authority 2026</p>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/p
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/p')`
5. The element will be highlighted

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://london.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-u-group u-space-x-2" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-u-group u-space-x-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-w-full btn btn--outline" href="/who-we-are">       View our who we are page   </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-w-full btn btn--outline"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are/what-mayor-does">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are" class="u-font-normal">               Who we are             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-font-normal"]`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R43](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r43)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg role="img" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R60](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r60)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The grouping element has an accessible name
- HTML: `<fieldset data-drupal-selector="edit-checkbox-mailchimp" id="edit-checkbox-mailchimp--wrapper" class="checkboxes--wrapper fieldgroup form-composite webform-composite-visible-title js-webform-type-checkboxes webform-type-checkboxes js-form-item form-item js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" aria-describedby="edit-checkbox-mailchimp--wrapper--description">...</fieldset>`
- XPath: `/fieldset[@id="edit-checkbox-mailchimp--wrapper"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 4.52:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="lead">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lead"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>© Copyright Greater London Authority 2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<iframe title="reCAPTCHA" width="304" height="78" role="presentation" name="a-2dfyfnhz3nri" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" sandbox="allow-forms allow-popups allow-same-origin allow-scripts allow-top-navigation allow-modals allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox allow-storage-access-by-user-activation" src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api2/anchor?ar=1&k=6Ld5PzEUAAAAAG34guiPpNoqPmNKMdrvJaeJO5Zl&co=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubG9uZG9uLmdvdi51azo0NDM.&hl=en&type=image&v=QvLuXwupqtKCyjBw2xIzFLIf&theme=light&size=normal&anchor-ms=20000&execute-ms=30000&cb=wlytedq2uuta" />`
- XPath: `/iframe`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

### https://london.gov.uk/find-us-facebook

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="x1i10hfl xjbqb8w x1ejq31n x18oe1m7 x1sy0etr xstzfhl x972fbf x10w94by x1qhh985 x14e42zd x9f619 x1ypdohk xt0psk2 x3ct3a4 xdj266r x14z9mp xat24cr x1lziwak xexx8yu xyri2b x18d9i69 x1c1uobl x16tdsg8 x1hl2dhg xggy1nq x1a2a7pz xkrqix3 x1sur9pj x1fey0fg x1s688f" href="https://www.facebook.com/recover/initiate?ars=royal_blue_bar" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Forgot Account?</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="x1i10hfl xjbqb8w x1ejq31n x18oe1m7 x1sy0etr xstzfhl x972fbf x10w94by x1qhh985 x14e42zd x9f619 x1ypdohk xt0psk2 x3ct3a4 xdj266r x14z9mp xat24cr x1lziwak xexx8yu xyri2b x18d9i69 x1c1uobl x16tdsg8 x1hl2dhg xggy1nq x1a2a7pz xkrqix3 x1sur9pj x1fey0fg x1s688f"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div aria-label="Log in to Facebook" class="x1i10hfl xjbqb8w x1ejq31n x18oe1m7 x1sy0etr xstzfhl x972fbf x10w94by x1qhh985 x14e42zd x1ypdohk x3ct3a4 xdj266r x14z9mp xat24cr x1lziwak xexx8yu xyri2b x18d9i69 x1c1uobl x16tdsg8 x1hl2dhg xggy1nq x1fmog5m xu25z0z x140muxe xo1y3bh x87ps6o x1lku1pv x1a2a7pz x9f619 x3nfvp2 xdt5ytf xl56j7k x1n2onr6 xh8yej3" role="button" tabindex="0">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="x1i10hfl xjbqb8w x1ejq31n x18oe1m7 x1sy0etr xstzfhl x972fbf x10w94by x1qhh985 x14e42zd x1ypdohk x3ct3a4 xdj266r x14z9mp xat24cr x1lziwak xexx8yu xyri2b x18d9i69 x1c1uobl x16tdsg8 x1hl2dhg xggy1nq x1fmog5m xu25z0z x140muxe xo1y3bh x87ps6o x1lku1pv x1a2a7pz x9f619 x3nfvp2 xdt5ytf xl56j7k x1n2onr6 xh8yej3"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="x1i10hfl xjbqb8w x1ejq31n x18oe1m7 x1sy0etr xstzfhl x972fbf x10w94by x1qhh985 x14e42zd x9f619 x1ypdohk xt0psk2 x3ct3a4 xdj266r x14z9mp xat24cr x1lziwak xexx8yu xyri2b x18d9i69 x1c1uobl x16tdsg8 x1hl2dhg xggy1nq x1a2a7pz xkrqix3 x1sur9pj x1qq9wsj x1s688f" href="https://www.facebook.com/recover/initiate?ars=royal_blue_bar" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">...</a>`

#### Rule: [SIA-R17](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)

- HTML: `<div class="x9f619 x1ja2u2z x1pq812k x5yr21d x1o0tod xw2csxc x1odjw0f xixxii4 x1rohswg x13vifvy xh8yej3 xfk6m8 x1yqm8si xjx87ck" aria-hidden="true" id="scrollview" style="left: 0px;">...</div>`

### https://london.gov.uk/warmer-homes-faqs/i-received-support-under-first-phase-warmer-homes-can-i-re-apply-phase-warmer-homes

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-u-group u-space-x-2" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-u-group u-space-x-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/warmer-homes-faqs/do-only-domestic-properties-qualify-scheme" hreflang="en">Do only domestic properties qualify for the scheme...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are" class="u-font-normal">               Who we are             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-font-normal"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a target="_blank" href="https://translate.google.com/" class="google-translate-icon" aria-label="powered by Google Translate" />`
- XPath: `/a[@class="google-translate-icon"]`

*... and 1 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R43](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r43)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg role="img" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)
**WCAG**: Best Practice

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h3 class="h3">                     Related questions            ...</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@class="h3"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h5 class="h5">                     Eligibility             </h5>`
- XPath: `/h5[@class="h5"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 4.52:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>© Copyright Greater London Authority 2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

- XPath: `/h5[@class="h5"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 4.52:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>© Copyright Greater London Authority 2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `lang` attribute is either missing, empty, or only whitespace
- HTML: `<html>...</html>`
- XPath: `/html`

### https://london.gov.uk/investigation-request-metropolitan-police-actions-against-university-london-students

#### Rule: [SIA-R96](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r96)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The refresh or redirect is delayed
- HTML: `<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="360" />`
- XPath: `/meta`

### https://london.gov.uk/reports-and-toolkits

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-u-group u-space-x-2" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-u-group u-space-x-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are" class="u-font-normal">               Who we are             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-font-normal"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a target="_blank" href="https://translate.google.com/" class="google-translate-icon" aria-label="powered by Google Translate" />`
- XPath: `/a[@class="google-translate-icon"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<select class="gt_selector notranslate" aria-label="Select Language">...</select>`
- XPath: `/select[@class="gt_selector notranslate"]`

*... and 1 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R43](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r43)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg role="img" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 4.52:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>© Copyright Greater London Authority 2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

- HTML: `<select class="gt_selector notranslate" aria-label="Select Language">...</select>`
- XPath: `/select[@class="gt_selector notranslate"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.london.gov.uk/google-translate-disclaimer">Translation disclaimer</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R43](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r43)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg role="img" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 4.52:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>© Copyright Greater London Authority 2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

- HTML: `<button class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-u-group u-space-x-2" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-u-group u-space-x-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are" class="u-font-normal">               Who we are             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-font-normal"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a target="_blank" href="https://translate.google.com/" class="google-translate-icon" aria-label="powered by Google Translate" />`
- XPath: `/a[@class="google-translate-icon"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<select class="gt_selector notranslate" aria-label="Select Language">...</select>`
- XPath: `/select[@class="gt_selector notranslate"]`

*... and 1 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R43](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r43)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg role="img" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin"]`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 4.52:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>© Copyright Greater London Authority 2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

### https://london.gov.uk/city-hall-blog/grenfell-tower-national-memorial-service

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-u-group u-space-x-2" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-u-group u-space-x-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="mailto:?body=Check%20out%20this%20site%20https%3A//www.london.gov.uk/city-hall-blog/grenfell-tower-national-memorial-service&subject=Grenfell%20Tower%20National%20Memorial%20service" target="_blank" rel="noopener" aria-label="Share via Email" data-sharer="email" :data-title="title" :data-subject="title" data-to="" data-title="Grenfell Tower National Memorial service \| London City Hall" data-subject="Grenfell Tower National Memorial service \| London City Hall">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are" class="u-font-normal">               Who we are             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-font-normal"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size

- XPath: `/a[@class="google-translate-icon"]`

- XPath: `/a[@class="u-u-group u-space-x-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="mailto:?body=Check%20out%20this%20site%20https%3A//www.london.gov.uk/events/mayors-christmas-carol-service-2023&subject=The%20Mayor%27s%20Christmas%20Carol%20Service%202023" target="_blank" rel="noopener" aria-label="Share via Email" data-sharer="email" :data-title="title" :data-subject="title" data-to="" data-title="The Mayor's Christmas Carol Service 2023 \| London City Hall" data-subject="The Mayor's Christmas Carol Service 2023 \| London City Hall">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are" class="u-font-normal">               Who we are             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-font-normal"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a target="_blank" href="https://translate.google.com/" class="google-translate-icon" aria-label="powered by Google Translate" />`
- XPath: `/a[@class="google-translate-icon"]`

- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-u-group u-space-x-2" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-u-group u-space-x-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#about-the-ceremony-297529-title" class="u-font-normal node-name--H2 u-ml-2 u-underline hover:u-text-current is-active-link">About the ceremony</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-font-normal node-name--H2 u-ml-2 u-underline hover:u-text-current is-active-link"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#watch-the-livestream-398042-title" class="u-font-normal node-name--H2 u-ml-2 u-underline hover:u-text-current">Watch the livestream</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-font-normal node-name--H2 u-ml-2 u-underline hover:u-text-current"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="mailto:?body=Check%20out%20this%20site%20https%3A//www.london.gov.uk/events/remembrance-service-2025&subject=Remembrance%20Service%202025" target="_blank" rel="noopener" aria-label="Share via Email" data-sharer="email" :data-title="title" :data-subject="title" data-to="" data-title="Remembrance Service 2025 \| London City Hall" data-subject="Remembrance Service 2025 \| London City Hall">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 id="key-info-heading" class="h2">                     Key information             </h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="key-info-heading"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://london.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [svg-img-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/svg-img-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text
- HTML: `<svg role="img" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin" focusable="false">`
- XPath: `.simple-icons-icon__linkedin`

### https://london.gov.uk/find-us-facebook

#### Rule: [aria-dialog-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-dialog-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA dialog and alertdialog nodes should have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div role="dialog" class="x1n2onr6 x1ja2u2z x1afcbsf x78zum5 xdt5ytf x1a2a7pz x6ikm8r x10wlt62 x71s49j x1jx94hy xw5cjc7 x1dmpuos x1vsv7so xau1kf4 x104qc98 x15o3w11 xogydr4 x1vmz7ll x1yyrj1m x193iq5w">`
- XPath: `.x1afcbsf`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA dialog and alertdialog nodes should have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div role="dialog" class="x1n2onr6 x1ja2u2z x1afcbsf x78zum5 xdt5ytf x1a2a7pz x6ikm8r x10wlt62 x71s49j x1jx94hy xw5cjc7 x1dmpuos x1vsv7so xau1kf4 x104qc98 x15o3w11 xogydr4 x1vmz7ll x1yyrj1m x193iq5w">`
- XPath: `.x1afcbsf`

#### Rule: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<span class="x1lliihq x6ikm8r x10wlt62 x1n2onr6 xlyipyv xuxw1ft">Create new account</span>`
- XPath: `.xv9rvxn > .x14ayic.xwyz465.x1e0frkt > .xsqbvy7.xb9jzoj[role="none"] > .x1lkfr7t.x1lbecb7.xtk6v10 > .xlyipyv.xuxw1ft.x6ikm8r`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<span class="x1lliihq x6ikm8r x10wlt62 x1n2onr6 xlyipyv xuxw1ft">Create new account</span>`
- XPath: `.xv9rvxn > .x14ayic.xwyz465.x1e0frkt > .xsqbvy7.xb9jzoj[role="none"] > .x1lkfr7t.x1lbecb7.xtk6v10 > .xlyipyv.xuxw1ft.x6ikm8r`

#### Rule: [meta-viewport-large](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/meta-viewport-large?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Users should be able to zoom and scale the text up to 500%
- HTML: `<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1,maximum-scale=2,shrink-to-fit=no">`
- XPath: `meta[name="viewport"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Users should be able to zoom and scale the text up to 500%
- HTML: `<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1,maximum-scale=2,shrink-to-fit=no">`
- XPath: `meta[name="viewport"]`

### https://london.gov.uk/find-advice-and-support

#### Rule: [meta-refresh](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/meta-refresh?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical
**WCAG**: [SC 2.2.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/timing-adjustable) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Delayed refresh under 20 hours must not be used
- HTML: `<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="360">`
- XPath: `meta[http-equiv="refresh"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Delayed refresh under 20 hours must not be used
- HTML: `<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="360">`
- XPath: `meta[http-equiv="refresh"]`

### https://london.gov.uk/warmer-homes-faqs/i-received-support-under-first-phase-warmer-homes-can-i-re-apply-phase-warmer-homes

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h3 class="h3">                     Related questions             </h3>`
- XPath: `.u-space-y-4 > h3`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h5 class="h5">                     Eligibility             </h5>`
- XPath: `.u-mb-10:nth-child(1) > .u-bg-off-white.u-p-6.sm\:u-px-12 > h5`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.4](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/resize-text) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Zooming and scaling must not be disabled
- HTML: `<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale = 1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, user-scalable=no">`
- XPath: `meta[name="viewport"]`

**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="top-row">`
- XPath: `.top-row`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div id="full-width-content">`
- XPath: `#full-width-content`
